### Shared Focuses ###
shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_black_monday
	icon = GFX_goal_HOL_black_monday
	x = 0
	y = 0
	
	
	cost = 4
	available = { has_idea = rus_black_monday }
	bypass = {
		has_idea = rus_black_monday
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_idea = RUS_civil_war_aftermath_idea
		}
	}
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000
	}
	
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus RUS_black_monday"
		add_political_power = 25
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_taxes
	icon = GFX_goal_CZE_income_tax
	cost = 4
	prerequisite = { focus = RUS_Drop_The_Gold_Standard }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = RUS_Nationalize_German_Assets }
	cancel_if_invalid = yes
	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS_kerensky_in_power = yes
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = russia_must_wait_unlock
				has_country_flag = unlock_economy
			}
		}
		hidden_trigger = { 
			has_country_flag = RUS_black_monday_senate_plan 
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_civil_war_will_happen }
		}
	}
	bypass = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_idea = RUS_civil_war_aftermath_idea
		}
	}
	relative_position_id = RUS_black_monday
	x = 1
	y = 2
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000
	}
	completion_reward = {
		add_political_power = 100
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_1
			add_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = russia.25 
		}
	}
}
shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_currency
	icon = GFX_focus_rus_ruble
	cost = 4   
	prerequisite = { 
		focus = RUS_Nationalize_German_Assets
		focus = RUS_taxes
	}
	relative_position_id = RUS_black_monday
	x = 0
	y = 3
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1000
	}
	available = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS_kerensky_in_power = yes
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = russia_must_wait_unlock
				has_country_flag = unlock_economy
			}
		}
		hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_civil_war_will_happen } }
	}
	cancel_if_invalid = yes
	bypass = {
		hidden_trigger = {
			has_idea = RUS_civil_war_aftermath_idea
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		add_stability = 0.025
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Nationalize_German_Assets
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_2
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_4
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_taxes
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_2
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_4
				}
			}
		}
		else = {		
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_Balance_The_Budget_tooltip
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_3
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_5
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_2
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_duma_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_3
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_5
				}
			}
			else = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_2
					add_idea = rus_black_monday_senate_4
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	}

		factor = 5
	}

		add_stability = 0.06
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 651 decision = RUS_Develop_Civilian_Industry_In_State } #Ufa
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 248 decision = RUS_Develop_Civilian_Industry_In_State } #Yaroslavl
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 252 decision = RUS_Develop_Civilian_Industry_In_State } #Nizhny Novgorod
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_Local_Development_tooltip

			limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_6 }
			swap_ideas = {

			}
		}
		else = {

			}
		}
	}

			}
		}

			limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_7 }

				remove_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_7

			}
		}

			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {

shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_War_Preparations_Programme
	icon = GFX_MON_army_money
	relative_position_id = RUS_Reinstitute_The_Zemstva
	x = 0
	y = 3
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = {
		focus = RUS_Local_Development
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 20
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus RUS_War_Preparations_Programme"		
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_War_Preparations_Programme_tooltip
		add_war_support = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = unlock_uztm} }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 653 decision = RUS_uralmash }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = unlock_chtz } }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 572 decision = RUS_chelyabinsk_tractor_plant }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		if = { #has research initiatives
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_3
				add_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_5
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has investment bank
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_7 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_7
				add_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_9
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has research initiatives and investment bank
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_8 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_new_zemstva_8

shared_focus = {
	id = RUS_Military_Production_Act
	icon = GFX_goal_NIC_Military_Industry
	relative_position_id = RUS_Bureaucratic_Overhaul
	x = -1
	y = 2
	cost = 5
	prerequisite = {
		focus = RUS_MinProm
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 20
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus RUS_Military_Production_Act"
		
		if = { #has agriculture
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_minprom_3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_minprom_3
				add_idea = RUS_minprom_6
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has efficiency
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_minprom_4 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_minprom_4
				add_idea = RUS_minprom_7
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has admin school
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_minprom_5 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_minprom_5
				add_idea = RUS_minprom_8
			}
		}
		else_if = { #has agriculture + efficiency
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_minprom_9 }

			date > 1939.1.1
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {

		RUS_decrease_volunteerism = yes
		add_mastery = {
			amount = 120
			track = infantry
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line

			limit = { has_idea = RUS_russian_army_i_5b }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_russian_army_i_5b
				add_idea = RUS_russian_army_i_7b
			}
		}
		else_if = { # cavalry corps
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_russian_army_i_4b }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_russian_army_i_4b
				add_idea = RUS_russian_army_i_8b
			}
		}
		else_if = { # cavalry corps + volunteer mobilization
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_russian_army_i_6b }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_russian_army_i_6b
				add_idea = RUS_russian_army_i_9b
			}
		}
		else = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_russian_army_i_2b
				add_idea = RUS_russian_army_i_3b
			}
		}
	}

				custom_override_tooltip = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = naval_facility

						province = 6174 #Petrograd
						instant_build = yes
					}
					tooltip = {
						localization_key = tooltip_add_building_on_victory_point
						BUILDING = naval_facility
						NUMBER = 1
						VP = 6174
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { extra_facility = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { free_building_slots = { building = dockyard size > 2 include_locked = yes } }
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { free_building_slots = { building = dockyard size > 1 include_locked = yes } }
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 2
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { extra_dockyards = 1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { free_building_slots = { building = dockyard size > 0 include_locked = yes } }
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_temp_variable = { extra_dockyards = 2 }
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { extra_dockyards = 3 }
			}
			custom_override_tooltip = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = naval_base
					level = 3
					province = 6174
					instant_build = yes
				}
				tooltip = {
					localization_key = tooltip_add_building_on_victory_point
					BUILDING = naval_base
					NUMBER = 3
					VP = 6174
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { extra_dockyards > 0 } }
			add_one_random_dockyard = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { extra_dockyards > 1 } }
			add_one_random_dockyard = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { extra_dockyards > 2 } }
			add_one_random_dockyard = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = extra_facility }
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					can_construct_building = naval_facility
				}
				construct_building_in_random_province = { naval_facility = 1 }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		set_country_flag = upgrade_bf
		set_country_flag = upgrade_av
		if = { #Tooltip for those that have MIOs
			limit = { has_dlc_aat = yes }
			mio:RUS_baltiysky_verfi_organisation = {
				add_mio_funds = 1000
				add_mio_size = 1
			}
			mio:RUS_admiralteiskie_verfi_organisation = {
				add_mio_funds = 1000
				add_mio_size = 1
			}
		}
		else = { #Tooltip for those that have vanilla companies
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = RUS_unlock_improved_company COMPANY = baltiysky_verfi
			}
			show_ideas_tooltip = baltiysky_verfi_improved
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = RUS_unlock_improved_company COMPANY = admiralteiskie_verfi
			}
			show_ideas_tooltip = admiralteiskie_verfi_improved
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = baltiysky_verfi }
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = baltiysky_verfi
						add_idea = baltiysky_verfi_improved
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = admiralteiskie_verfi }
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = admiralteiskie_verfi
						add_idea = admiralteiskie_verfi_improved
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
